#Sending:
vu_send_administrative_bureaucrats_for_ADM = {
	category = economy

	require_acceptance = yes #Set to no so that this is a player to player and or ai interaction. - SF

	is_visible = {
	    ROOT = {
		   ai = no
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		ROOT = {
			adm_power = 25
			has_opinion = { #This is opinion of sender towards receiver
				who = FROM
				value = 25
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			owes_favors = {
				who = ROOT
				value = 10
			}
		}
		NOT = { #Don addition
			has_country_flag = vu_send_administrative_bureaucrats_for_adm_flag
		}
		if = { #Don addition
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = vu_send_administrative_bureaucrats_for_adm_cooldown_flag
			}
			had_country_flag = { #Is the effect
				flag = vu_send_administrative_bureaucrats_for_adm_cooldown_flag
				days = 1825
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		clr_country_flag = vu_send_administrative_bureaucrats_for_adm_cooldown_flag #Don addition
		set_country_flag = vu_send_administrative_bureaucrats_for_adm_flag
		set_country_flag = vu_send_administrative_bureaucrats_for_adm_cooldown_flag #Don addition
		clr_country_flag = vu_send_diplomatic_envoys_for_dip_flag
		clr_country_flag = vu_send_military_attaches_for_mil_flag
		#Yeeted ROOT because it is already in ROOT
		add_adm_power = -25
		add_treasury = -10   #State paid transportation fees for the Bureaucrats.
		add_favors = {
			who = FROM
			amount = 10
		}
		add_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = sought_25_bureaucratic_adm_points
		}
		FROM = {
			add_adm_power = 25
			add_favors = {
		    	who = ROOT
		    	amount = -10
		    }
			add_trust = {
				who = ROOT
				value = 5
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = provided_25_bureaucratic_adm_points
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
		add_prestige = -10
		add_treasury = 10   #Reimbursement of state paid transportation fees for the Bureaucrats.
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = Don_is_a_TWAT
            
            # Restricts this entry to the countries that validate the triggers. Optional.
            #limit = {
            #    always = yes
            #}

            export_to_variable = {
                variable_name = ai_value
                value = modifier:diplomatic_reputation
                who = FROM
                with = THIS
            }
            
            # You can then change ai_value with effects such as multiply_variable, etc
        }
    }

	ai_will_do = { #Ai stuff by DonBrom
		alliance_with = FROM
		trust = {
			who = FROM
			value = 70
		}
		has_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			value = 150
		}
		treasury = 250
		is_at_war = no
		has_any_disaster = no
		is_in_deficit = no
		is_month = 11 #Don's a genius and I love it! December = Winter is coming. :P
		adm_power = 750
		is_great_power = yes #Another Don addition - If you're a shitty tag then forget it! xD
		FROM = {
			ai = no
			is_subject = no #Another Don addition - Subjects don't get it! xD
			is_great_power = no # xD
			OR = {
				is_at_war = yes
				has_any_disaster = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

vu_send_diplomatic_envoys_for_DIP = {
	category = economy

	require_acceptance = yes #Set to no so that this is a player to player and or ai interaction. - SF

	is_visible = {
	    ROOT = {
		   ai = no
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		ROOT = {
			dip_power = 25
			diplomatic_reputation = 1 #Prussia contribution - SF
			has_opinion = { #This is opinion of sender towards receiver
				who = FROM
				value = 25
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			owes_favors = {
				who = ROOT
				value = 10
			}
		}
		NOT = { #Don addition
			has_country_flag = vu_send_diplomatic_envoys_for_dip_flag
		}
		if = { #Don addition
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = vu_send_diplomatic_envoys_for_dip_cooldown_flag
			}
			had_country_flag = { #Is the effect
				flag = vu_send_diplomatic_envoys_for_dip_cooldown_flag
				days = 1825
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		clr_country_flag = vu_send_diplomatic_envoys_for_dip_cooldown_flag #Don addition
		set_country_flag = vu_send_diplomatic_envoys_for_dip_flag
		set_country_flag = vu_send_diplomatic_envoys_for_dip_cooldown_flag #Don addition
		clr_country_flag = vu_send_administrative_bureaucrats_for_adm_flag
		clr_country_flag = vu_send_military_attaches_for_mil_flag
		#Yeeted ROOT because it is already in ROOT
		add_dip_power = -25
		add_treasury = -10   #State paid transportation fees for the Envoys.
		add_favors = {
			who = FROM
			amount = 10
		}
		add_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = sought_25_diplomatic_dip_points
		}
		FROM = {
			add_dip_power = 25
			add_favors = {
		    	who = ROOT
		    	amount = -10
		    }
			add_trust = {
				who = ROOT
				value = 5
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = provided_25_diplomatic_dip_points
			}

		}
	}
	on_decline = {
		add_prestige = -10
		add_treasury = 10   #Reimbursement of state paid transportation fees for the Envoys.
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = Don_is_a_TWAT
            
            # Restricts this entry to the countries that validate the triggers. Optional.
            #limit = {
            #    always = yes
            #}

            export_to_variable = {
                variable_name = ai_value
                value = modifier:diplomatic_reputation
                who = FROM
                with = THIS
            }
            
            # You can then change ai_value with effects such as multiply_variable, etc
        }
    }

	ai_will_do = { #Ai stuff by DonBrom
		alliance_with = FROM
		trust = {
			who = FROM
			value = 70
		}
		has_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			value = 150
		}
		treasury = 250
		is_at_war = no
		has_any_disaster = no
		is_in_deficit = no
		is_month = 11 #Don's a genius and I love it! December = Winter is coming. :P
		dip_power = 750
		is_great_power = yes #Another Don addition - If you're a shitty tag then forget it! xD
		FROM = {
			ai = no
			is_subject = no #Another Don addition - Subjects don't get it! xD
			is_great_power = no # xD
			OR = {
				is_at_war = yes
				has_any_disaster = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

vu_send_military_attaches_for_MIL = {
	category = economy

	require_acceptance = yes #Set to no so that this is a player to player and or ai interaction. - SF

	is_visible = {
	    ROOT = {
		   ai = no
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		ROOT = {
			mil_power = 25
			OR = {
				army_tradition = 10 #Prussia contribution - SF
				navy_tradition = 10 #Prussia contribution - SF
			}
			has_opinion = { #This is opinion of sender towards receiver
				who = FROM
				value = 25
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			owes_favors = {
				who = ROOT
				value = 10
			}
		}
		NOT = { #Don addition
			has_country_flag = vu_send_military_attaches_for_mil_flag
		}
		if = { #Don addition
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = vu_send_military_attaches_for_mil_cooldown_flag
			}
			had_country_flag = { #Is the effect
				flag = vu_send_military_attaches_for_mil_cooldown_flag
				days = 1825
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		clr_country_flag = vu_send_military_attaches_for_mil_cooldown_flag #Don addition
		set_country_flag = vu_send_military_attaches_for_mil_flag
		set_country_flag = vu_send_military_attaches_for_mil_cooldown_flag #Don addition
		clr_country_flag = vu_send_administrative_bureaucrats_for_adm_flag
		clr_country_flag = vu_send_diplomatic_envoys_for_dip_flag
		#Yeeted ROOT because it is already in ROOT
		add_mil_power = -25
		add_treasury = -10   #State paid transportation fees for the Attaches.
		add_favors = {
			who = FROM
			amount = 10
		}
		add_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			modifier = sought_25_military_mil_points
		}
		FROM = {
			add_mil_power = 25
			add_favors = {
		    	who = ROOT
		    	amount = -10
		    }
			add_trust = {
				who = ROOT
				value = 5
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = provided_25_military_mil_points
			}

		}
	}
	on_decline = {
		add_prestige = -10
		add_treasury = 10   #Reimbursement of state paid transportation fees for the Attaches.
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = Don_is_a_TWAT
            
            # Restricts this entry to the countries that validate the triggers. Optional.
            #limit = {
            #    always = yes
            #}

            export_to_variable = {
                variable_name = ai_value
                value = modifier:diplomatic_reputation
                who = FROM
                with = THIS
            }
            
            # You can then change ai_value with effects such as multiply_variable, etc
        }
    }

	ai_will_do = { #Ai stuff by DonBrom
		alliance_with = FROM
		trust = {
			who = FROM
			value = 70
		}
		has_opinion = {
			who = FROM
			value = 150
		}
		treasury = 250
		is_at_war = no
		has_any_disaster = no
		is_in_deficit = no
		is_month = 11 #Don's a genius and I love it! December = Winter is coming. :P
		mil_power = 750
		is_great_power = yes #Another Don addition - If you're a shitty tag then forget it! xD

			is_great_power = no # xD

				is_at_war = yes

			}
		}

#New VU v1.37 additions by SF & Prussia
#ANGEVIN
promote_vassal_to_anglois_lordship = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_anglois_lordship_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_anglois_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = anglois_lordship
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_anglois_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM

				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {

				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4

rein_in_anglois_lordship = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_anglois_lordship_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_anglois_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = anglois_lordship
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 15
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 2
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = anglois_barony
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_barony_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_anglois_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

promote_vassal_to_anglois_barony = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_anglois_barony_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_anglois_barony
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 15
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 2
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = anglois_barony
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_barony_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_anglois_barony_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT

				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {

				value = -1
			}
		}
	}

rein_in_anglois_marquisate = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_anglois_marquisate_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_anglois_marquisate
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = anglois_marquisate
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 85
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 6
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = anglois_duchy
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_duchy_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_anglois_marquisate_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_barony_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_aragonese_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

promote_vassal_to_aragonese_barony = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_aragonese_barony_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_aragonese_barony
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 15
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 2
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = aragonese_barony
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_barony_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_aragonese_barony_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_aragonese_barony = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_aragonese_barony_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_aragonese_barony
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = aragonese_barony
		}
	}

		FROM = {
			total_development = 25

				liberty_desire = 50
			}

				}

				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_aragonese_marquisate
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = aragonese_marquisate
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 85
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 6
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = aragonese_duchy
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_duchy_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_aragonese_marquisate_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

		has_government_attribute = has_austrian_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}

		create_subject = {
			subject_type = austrian_lordship
			subject = FROM

					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}

					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_austrian_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag

		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}

promote_vassal_to_austrian_barony = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_austrian_barony_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_austrian_barony
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 15
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 2
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = austrian_barony
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_barony_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_austrian_barony_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

	alert_index = 5

				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag

			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4

		}

				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}

promote_vassal_to_austrian_duchy = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_austrian_duchy_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_austrian_duchy
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 120
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 6
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = austrian_duchy
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_duchy_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_austrian_duchy_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_austrian_duchy = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_austrian_duchy_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_austrian_duchy
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = austrian_duchy
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 170
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 7
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = austrian_principality
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_principality_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_austrian_duchy_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {

		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }

		}

					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }

					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_baltic_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag

		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}

		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT

			}

rein_in_baltic_barony = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_baltic_barony_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_baltic_barony
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = baltic_barony
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 25
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 3
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = baltic_viscounty
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_viscounty_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_baltic_barony_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_baltic_duchy = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_baltic_duchy_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_baltic_duchy
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = baltic_duchy
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 170
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 7
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = baltic_principality
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_principality_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_baltic_duchy_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {

				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4

				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }

				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}

	}

	}

			subject_type = belgian_principality
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_principality_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_belgian_duchy_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

promote_vassal_to_bohemian_lordship = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_bohemian_lordship_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_bohemian_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = bohemian_lordship
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_bohemian_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT

				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT

			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}

			}

promote_vassal_to_bohemian_viscounty = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_bohemian_viscounty_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_bohemian_viscounty
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 30
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 3
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = bohemian_viscounty
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_viscounty_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_bohemian_viscounty_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_bohemian_viscounty = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_bohemian_viscounty_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_bohemian_viscounty
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = bohemian_viscounty
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 35
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 4
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = bohemian_county
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_county_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_bohemian_viscounty_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

promote_vassal_to_bohemian_principality = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_bohemian_principality_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_bohemian_principality
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 240
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 7
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = bohemian_principality
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_principality_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_bohemian_principality_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_bohemian_principality = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_bohemian_principality_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_bohemian_principality
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = bohemian_principality
		}
	}
		is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 340
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 8
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = bohemian_kingdom
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_kingdom_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_bohemian_principality_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT

				value = 0.2

				with = ROOT

				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}

promote_vassal_to_burgundian_lordship = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_burgundian_lordship_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_burgundian_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = burgundian_lordship
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_burgundian_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}

				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2

				with = ROOT

				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4

				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}

				who = FROM

				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}

rein_in_burgundian_viscounty = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_burgundian_viscounty_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_burgundian_viscounty
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = burgundian_viscounty
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 35
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 4
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = burgundian_county
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_county_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_burgundian_viscounty_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_burgundian_principality = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_burgundian_principality_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_burgundian_principality
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = burgundian_principality
		}
	}
		is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 340
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 8
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = burgundian_kingdom
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_kingdom_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_burgundian_principality_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

#BYZANTINE
promote_vassal_to_byzantine_lordship = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_byzantine_lordship_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_byzantine_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = byzantine_lordship
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_byzantine_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_byzantine_viscounty_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {

			export_to_variable = {

				who = FROM

			}

promote_vassal_to_byzantine_county = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_byzantine_county_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_byzantine_county
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 45
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 4
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = byzantine_county
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_county_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_byzantine_county_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI

				value = 50

			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4

					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_kingdom_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_byzantine_principality_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {

			export_to_variable = {

				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}

#CASTILIAN
promote_vassal_to_castilian_lordship = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_castilian_lordship_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_castilian_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = castilian_lordship
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_castilian_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 45
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 4
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = castilian_county
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_county_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_castilian_county_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_castilian_county = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_castilian_county_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_castilian_county
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = castilian_county
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 70
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 5
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = castilian_marquisate
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_marquisate_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_castilian_county_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_castilian_kingdom_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_castilian_kingdom
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 480
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 8
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = castilian_kingdom
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_kingdom_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_castilian_kingdom_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

#DANISH
promote_vassal_to_danish_lordship = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_danish_lordship_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_danish_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = danish_lordship
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_danish_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_danish_lordship = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_danish_lordship_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_danish_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = danish_lordship
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 15
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 2
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = danish_barony
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_barony_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_danish_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

#DUTCH
promote_vassal_to_dutch_lordship = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_dutch_lordship_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_dutch_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = dutch_lordship
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_dutch_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_dutch_lordship = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_dutch_lordship_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_dutch_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = dutch_lordship
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 15
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 2
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = dutch_barony
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_barony_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_dutch_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
