promote_vassal_to_dutch_marquisate = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_dutch_marquisate_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_dutch_marquisate
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 60
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 5
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = dutch_marquisate
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_marquisate_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_dutch_marquisate_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}

		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM

				value = 50
			}

			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}

rein_in_english_lordship = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_english_lordship_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_english_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = english_lordship
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 10
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 2
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = english_barony
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_barony_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_english_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

promote_vassal_to_english_barony = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_english_barony_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_english_barony
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 20
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 2
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = english_barony
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_barony_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_english_barony_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM

				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {

				who = FROM

rein_in_english_marquisate = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_english_marquisate_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_english_marquisate
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = english_marquisate
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 50
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 6
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = english_duchy
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_duchy_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_english_marquisate_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {

            name = DIPLO_OPPINION

				with = ROOT

				value = 50

			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4

			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = french_lordship
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_french_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI

	ai_acceptance = {

				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_french_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

promote_vassal_to_french_barony = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_french_barony_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_french_barony
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 15
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 2
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = french_barony
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_barony_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_french_barony_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_duchy_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_french_marquisate_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

promote_vassal_to_french_duchy = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_french_duchy_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_french_duchy
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 120
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 6
	}

			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}

				}
				else = {

				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_french_duchy_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4

				which = ai_value

			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}

					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }

					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_german_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag

		}
	}

	}

		government_rank = 2
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = german_barony
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_barony_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_german_barony_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_german_barony = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_german_barony_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_german_barony
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = german_barony
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 25
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 3
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = german_viscounty
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_viscounty_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_german_barony_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION

				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT

				value = 0.2

				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}

		has_government_attribute = has_german_duchy
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 120
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 6
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = german_duchy
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_duchy_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_german_duchy_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_german_duchy = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_german_duchy_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_german_duchy
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = german_duchy
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 170
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 7
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = german_principality
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_principality_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_german_duchy_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

#HUNGARIAN
promote_vassal_to_hungarian_lordship = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_hungarian_lordship_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_hungarian_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = hungarian_lordship
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_hungarian_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4

				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE

rein_in_hungarian_barony = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_hungarian_barony_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_hungarian_barony
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = hungarian_barony
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 25
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 3
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = hungarian_viscounty
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_viscounty_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_hungarian_barony_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {

				value = -1
			}
		}

rein_in_hungarian_duchy = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_hungarian_duchy_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_hungarian_duchy
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = hungarian_duchy
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 170
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 7
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = hungarian_principality
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_principality_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_hungarian_duchy_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}

				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}

			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}

				which = ai_value
				value = 4

		}

				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM

				value = -1
			}

promote_vassal_to_italian_viscounty = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_italian_viscounty_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_italian_viscounty
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 30
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 3
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = italian_viscounty
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_viscounty_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_italian_viscounty_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT

			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}

				value = -1
			}
		}
	}

			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4

				which = ai_value

				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}

promote_vassal_to_italian_principality = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_italian_principality_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_italian_principality
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 240
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 7
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = italian_principality
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_principality_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_italian_principality_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_italian_principality = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_italian_principality_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_italian_principality
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = italian_principality
		}
	}
		is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 340
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 8
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = italian_kingdom
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_kingdom_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_italian_principality_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

#MONGOLIAN
promote_vassal_to_mongolian_vassal = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_mongolian_vassal_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_mongolian_vassal
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = mongolian_vassal
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = steppe_horde
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_mongolian_vassal_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT

				value = 50

			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4

				which = ai_value

	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_norwegian_viscounty_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_norwegian_viscounty
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 30
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 3
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = norwegian_viscounty
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }

					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}

					add_government_reform = eue_viscounty_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_norwegian_viscounty_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_norwegian_duchy_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

promote_vassal_to_norwegian_principality = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_norwegian_principality_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_norwegian_principality
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 240
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 7
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = norwegian_principality
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_principality_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_norwegian_principality_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}

				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2

				who = FROM
				with = ROOT

			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}

promote_vassal_to_polish_lordship = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_polish_lordship_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_polish_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = polish_lordship
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_polish_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT

				value = 50

			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {

				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4

	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = polish_principality
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_principality_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_polish_principality_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
		is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 340
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 8
	}

			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}

				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag

			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4

promote_vassal_to_portuguese_lordship = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_portuguese_lordship_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_portuguese_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = portuguese_lordship
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_portuguese_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}

rein_in_portuguese_viscounty = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_portuguese_viscounty_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_portuguese_viscounty
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = portuguese_viscounty
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 35
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 4
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = portuguese_county
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_county_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_portuguese_viscounty_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

promote_vassal_to_portuguese_county = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_portuguese_county_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_portuguese_county
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 45
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 4
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = portuguese_county
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_county_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_portuguese_county_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_portuguese_principality = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_portuguese_principality_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_portuguese_principality
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = portuguese_principality
		}
	}
		is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 340
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 8
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = portuguese_kingdom
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_kingdom_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_portuguese_principality_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

#PRUSSIAN
promote_vassal_to_prussian_lordship = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_prussian_lordship_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_prussian_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = prussian_lordship
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_prussian_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}

				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}

			export_to_variable = {

				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}

		}

promote_vassal_to_prussian_county = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_prussian_county_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_prussian_county
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 45
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 4
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = prussian_county
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_county_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_prussian_county_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_prussian_county = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_prussian_county_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_prussian_county
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = prussian_county
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 70
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 5
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = prussian_marquisate
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_marquisate_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_prussian_county_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {

				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM

        }

			}

#RUSSIAN
promote_vassal_to_russian_lordship = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_russian_lordship_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_russian_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = russian_lordship
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_russian_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_russian_lordship = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_russian_lordship_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_russian_lordship

		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {

			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 2
	}

				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

rein_in_russian_county = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_russian_county_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_russian_county
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = russian_county
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 70
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 5
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = russian_marquisate
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_marquisate_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_russian_county_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_kingdom_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_russian_kingdom_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}

#SWEDISH
promote_vassal_to_swedish_lordship = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_swedish_lordship_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_swedish_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = swedish_lordship
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_lordship_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_swedish_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_swedish_lordship = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_swedish_lordship_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_swedish_lordship
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = swedish_lordship
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 15
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 2
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = swedish_barony
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_barony_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_swedish_lordship_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION

				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}

		government_rank = 5
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = swedish_marquisate
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = eue_marquisate_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_swedish_county_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION

				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4

	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_islamic_imamate_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_islamic_imamate
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = FROM_IS_REBELLIOUS_TT
				FROM = { liberty_desire = 50 }
			}
		}
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = islamic_imamate
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = islamic_imamate_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_islamic_imamate_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

rein_in_islamic_imamate = {
	category = influence

	alert_index = 5
	alert_tooltip = rein_in_islamic_imamate_alert_tooltip

	require_acceptance = yes

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_islamic_imamate
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = islamic_imamate
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 15
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 2
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = islamic_grand_muftate
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = islamic_grand_muftate_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_rein_in_islamic_imamate_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
