#Islamic Emirate - 5
promote_vassal_to_islamic_emirate = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_islamic_emirate_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_islamic_emirate
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 60
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 5
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = islamic_emirate
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				else = {
					add_government_reform = islamic_emirate_reform
				}
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_islamic_emirate_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

#Islamic Governate - 5
promote_vassal_to_islamic_governate = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_islamic_governate_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		OR = {
			tag = MUG
			tag = TIM
			tag = YUA
		}
		#has_government_attribute = has_islamic_governate
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 5
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = islamic_governate
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				add_government_reform = islamic_governate_reform
				change_religion = PREV
				kill_heir = {}
				kill_ruler = yes
				define_ruler = {
					dynasty = overlord
					religion = PREV
				}
				add_legitimacy = 100
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_islamic_governate_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = yes	#There is never a reason for the Ottomans to not want to integrate their eyalets
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

#Islamic Malikate - 8
promote_vassal_to_islamic_malikate = {
	category = influence

	require_acceptance = yes

	alert_index = 6
	alert_tooltip = promote_vassal_to_islamic_malikate_alert_tooltip

	is_visible = {
		has_government_attribute = has_islamic_malikate
		FROM = {
			is_subject_of = ROOT
			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}
	is_allowed = {
		FROM = {
			total_development = 480
			NOT = {
				liberty_desire = 50
			}
		}
		government_rank = 8
	}
	on_accept = {
		create_subject = {
			subject_type = islamic_malikate
			subject = FROM
			keep_liberty_desire = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_reform = papacy_reform }
					NOT = { has_reform = celestial_empire }
					NOT = { has_reform = shogunate }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { government = monarchy } }
					change_government = monarchy
				}
				add_government_reform = islamic_malikate_reform
				change_religion = PREV
				kill_heir = {}
				kill_ruler = yes
				define_ruler = {
					dynasty = overlord
					religion = PREV
				}
				add_legitimacy = 100
				set_country_flag = has_promote_to_islamic_malikate_color
				set_country_flag = has_overriden_color_flag
				change_country_color = { country = ROOT }
			}
		}
	}
	on_decline = {
	}

	ai_will_do = { # this is a trigger
		always = no	#Too risky to test this out with the AI
	}

	ai_acceptance = {
        add_entry = {
            name = DIPLO_OPPINION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = opinion
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value 
				value = 0.2
			}
        }
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_TRUST_TOWARDS_ROOT
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trust
				who = FROM
				with = ROOT
			}			
			subtract_variable = { 
				which = ai_value
				value = 50
			}
			#1 trust = +4 ai points
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 0.4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_DIPLOMATIC_REPUTATION
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = trigger_value:diplomatic_reputation
			}
			#1 rep = 4
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = 4
			}
		}
		add_entry = {
			name = AI_LIBERTY_DESIRE
			export_to_variable = {
				variable_name = ai_value
				value = liberty_desire
				who = FROM
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = ai_value
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

			is_subject_of_type = vassal
		}
	}

			is_subject_of = ROOT

		}

		FROM = {
			total_development = 120

				liberty_desire = 50
			}
